Sokoban is a type of transport puzzle, in which the player pushes boxes or crates around in a warehouse, trying to get them to storage locations. The game is played on a board of squares, where each square is a floor or a wall. Some floor squares contain boxes, and some floor squares are marked as storage locations. \r\n\r\nThe player is confined to the board, and may move horizontally or vertically onto empty squares (never through walls or boxes). (Multi-play games are offered in \"Triple Play\", \"Five Play\", \"Ten Play\", \"Fifty Play\" and \"One Hundred Play\" versions.) \r\n\r\nIn games which do not have a wild card a player on average will receive the rare four-of-a-kind hand approximately once every 500 hands, while a player may play tens of thousands of hands before an extremely rare royal flush, which usually has the highest payout. \r\n\r\n\"Jacks or Better,\" sometimes simply called \"Draw Poker,\" is the most common variation of video poker.
